Templar
Affiliation
Templar Order
(formerly)
Inquisition
Location
Haven
Skyhold
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Mattrin
is a former
templar
recruit who joined the
Inquisition
after being rescued by Inquisition forces.
Background
Mattrin used to be a
Templar
recruit. When the senior members of the Order attended the
Divine Conclave
in the
Temple of Sacred Ashes
, the lower-ranking templars remained outside its grounds. As a result, they survived the opening of
the Breach
. In the aftermath Mattrin and fellow Templar
Lysette
found themselves besieged by
demons
, but were rescued by the Inquisition forces and brought to the safety of
Haven
.
Involvement
Mattrin can be found in the military camp outside
Haven
. In a
conversation with Lysette
, he tries to convince her that they cannot stay with the Inquisition. Although his companion argues that the Templar Order is in disarray, and no longer serving its purpose, Mattrin remains skeptical.
Despite his objections, Mattrin continues to follow the Inquisition. After the
destruction of Haven
and relocation to
Skyhold
, he can occasionally be seen wandering around the fortress.
Trivia
Mattrin shares the same name and occupation as
Ellendra
's lover, as witnessed via the following
note
.

Maura

This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.

the Herald
encounters her, she asks them to retrieve the ring stolen by the Templars.
When the ring is returned, she thanks the Herald for putting her husband's soul to rest.

.
Background
He was born and raised in
Denerim
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
The
Inquisitor
finds the Mercenary Captain in the Royal Quarters after defeating demons and
Venatori
. Once untied, the Mercenary tells them that Grand Duke Gaspard hired him and his men because he lacked enough
chevaliers
, offering them triple pay to move in on the palace at night as part of a coup. However, the Mercenary and his men were then lured into a trap by
Florianne de Chalons
, left to be killed by demons. The Mercenary believes that Gaspard masterminded the trap with his sister to avoid paying his bill.
The Inquisitor can recruit him as an agent to testify against Grand Duke Gaspard.

======================================================================
PAGE: Merchant (Skyhold) (invisible)
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Merchant_(Skyhold)_(invisible)
======================================================================

Character
Invisible Merchant
Title
Merchant
Affiliation
Inquisition
Location
Skyhold
Quests
Opening the Roads
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
The so-called
"Invisible Merchant"
is a
merchant
in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
; the stall can be found in
Skyhold
.
Background
This merchant sells
weapons
, weapon
upgrades
,
armors
,
crafting materials
, weapon
schematics
, weapon upgrade schematics,
armor schematics
and
recipes
in
Skyhold
. The merchant is located in the lower courtyard near the Skyhold stables and fast travel marker. The stall can be found just to the left of
Farris The Representative
.
Involvement
The Invisible Merchant's stall and wares are unlocked and will appear in Skyhold following the completion of the
war table
operation
Opening the Roads
. There is not an actual character added upon completion of the operation.
Note:
The Invisible Merchant's stall represents a satellite operation for merchants found across
Thedas
. Only one merchant's wares are represented at any given time. Each time Skyhold is entered or a game is loaded the merchant represented is randomly selected. If all of a particular merchant's items have been purchased, the Invisible Merchant will represent the merchant in the same fashion without any wares.
Quests
Opening the Roads
(war table)
Merchants represented
One of the following merchants is selected at random to be represented by the Invisible Merchant:
Caer Bronach Merchant
Village of Crestwood Merchant
Gertrude
Suledin Keep Merchant
Master Taniel
Crossroads Merchant
Dwarven Bookseller
Redcliffe Armor & Upgrades Merchant
Redcliffe Weapons & Upgrades Merchant
Canyon Merchant
Barnabus
Havel
Pierre-Marie
Saphi
Val Royeaux Expensive Merchant
Val Royeaux Schematics Merchant
Val Royeaux Weapons & Upgrades Merchant
Griffon Wing Keep Merchant
Note:
Merchants that are excluded from being represented include: all Skyhold merchants,
Deraboam
the
Mystery Box
merchant, the
Skyhold Customization Merchant
from
Val Royeaux
,
Willvan
the Codex merchant, and all merchants added from
downloadable content
.
Special offers
With the acquisition of
the Short List
Inquisition
perk
, additional items are added as special offers. These offers are available randomly each time the Inquisitor enters the map. If any special offers are available only one offer will be available at a time. The offer will always be listed first in its category.
Bugs
The Short List
Inquisition
perk
seems to have an unexpected interaction with the
war table
operation
Opening the Roads
. The operation must be completed prior to obtaining the perk thus allowing for the merchant's stall to physically appear in Skyhold. If the perk is acquired prior to completing the operation, then the merchant's stall will remain invisible indefinitely, and may also potentially prevent the merchant's wares from being interacted with.

======================================================================
PAGE: Michel de Chevin
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters, Dragon Age: The Masked Empire characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Michel_de_Chevin
======================================================================

“The Academie gave me my honor, and the peace of knowing that as long as I am true to it, I may die with a happy heart.”
Character
Michel de Chevin
Title
Chevalier
Champion of
Celene I
(formerly)
Inquisition Agent
(conditional)
Race
Human
(
Elf-blooded
)
Gender
Male
Class
Warrior
Affiliation
Inquisition
(conditional)
Location
Sahrnia
,
Emprise du Lion
Skyhold
(conditional)
Quests
Call Me Imshael
Capturing Suledin Keep
Assigning Michel de Chevin
(conditional)
Reconciliation for Celene and Michel
(conditional)
Restoring Michel de Chevin's Honor
(conditional)
(conditional)
Voice
Damian Lynch
Appearances
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Heroes of Dragon Age
Ser
Michel de Chevin
is a
chevalier
and champion of
Empress
Celene I
. A
warrior
skilled in all forms of combat, he also deeply values the chevalier code of honor. He was sponsored into the
Academie des Chevaliers
by Comte Brevin de Chalons, with whom Ser Michel was fostered as a youth.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
.
Michel is the bastard
elf-blooded
son of an
elven
mother and a
human
commoner father.
He grew up in the
alienage
of Montfort with his mother and she provided for him by working in a
tavern
.
Michel's life was one of poverty and fear, for the chevaliers would often kill peasants in the slums.
His mother died when he was a child. When he was ten, Comte Brevin de Chalons saw him fighting off three larger boys in an alley to save a friend and ordered his coach to stop and help. Brevin took Michel in to train with his family's guards and after three years, paid an expert in
heraldry
and legal documents,
le Mage du Sang
, to make up a title for him.
Ever since Michel posed as Ser Michel de Chevin, a distant cousin to the de Chevins, coming from a dead line of the family so that his assumed identity could not be questioned.
Brevin also paid for his induction into the Academie des Chevaliers which accepted only those of noble birth; Michel arrived at the Academie with a letter of introduction from Comte Guy
de Montfort
confirming his lineage. The years in the Academie were the best in his life and he excelled in the martial training. For a final trial, he and the other senior students were taken to the slums after dark to "test their blades" by killing elves.
Michel eventually rose to the position of
Empress
Celene's
champion after her previous one died stopping an assassination attempt and has served her faithfully for nearly ten years.
Involvement
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
.
The plot follows BioWare's own canon
, meaning it may not follow some of the player's choices in the games.
Ser Michel accompanies Empress Celene to meet with Chancelier Morrac of the
University of Orlais
regarding the acceptance of promising commoners and elves who can obtain sponsorship for their applications. Celene suggests that elves are already present at the university, and unwittingly asks an understandably reluctant Michel to identify a mural of the elven
Disciple
Shartan
that had been subjected to iconoclasm following the
Exalted March
of the
Dales
. He then escorts Celene to a meeting with
Divine
Justinia
's representative,
Leliana
.
Later on, at a ball hosted by Empress Celene, Grand Duke
Gaspard de Chalons
attempts to goad
Teagan Guerrin
, the
Fereldan
ambassador, into a duel by insulting
Moira Theirin
's memory. Celene, however, outwits him by offering her own champion, Ser Michel, in the duel to satisfy Teagan, and Ferelden's, honor. The challenged party has the choice of weapon, and Ser Michel at Celene's behest chooses a feather as the weapon of choice (more specifically the feather of the chevaliers). This harmlessly settles the debt to the delight of some and the outrage of others.
The next morning
Melcendre
, a
bard
in Gaspard's employ who had assisted him at the ball the previous night, lures Ser Michel to a tavern in the slums with a note. She attacks him backed by six armed men and manages to neutralize him with choking dust which was based on
deep mushrooms
. Michel is brought to a warehouse in the alienage of
Val Royeaux
. Melcendre comes to the warehouse and reveals that she has learned of his past and his elven heritage. Only those of noble blood are allowed into the ranks of the chevaliers and Michel is a commoner and, worse, elf-blooded, information that would disgrace the Empress and destroy his life if revealed. Melcendre intends to provide the information to Gaspard, but Michel knocks her down and strangles her before killing her with her own dagger. Just as Michel is confronted by a group of Gaspard's soldiers,
Briala
and
Felassan
appear and help him escape.
During the escape Briala deduces from the chevalier's reactions to the word "knife-ear", something he'd never said to her or any other servant, that Michel is elf-blooded. Briala tells Michel that she will never tell anyone about his secret, but that he now owes her one favor that she can call in at any time. Although Michel has no idea what that favor will be, he accepts the deal to protect his status as a chevalier and also as Celene's champion.
Michel later escorts Empress Celene to a play at the Grande Royeaux Theater aimed to weaken her political position by painting her as overly sympathetic to the elves, at a time when the elven slums of
Halamshiral
are rebelling. This leads Celene to order Michel and her forces to march on the city to crush the rebellion and cement her strength in the eyes of the nobility. Celene orders Halamshiral to be burned down while the elves are still inside the city.
When Michel, Celene, Briala and Felassan later become trapped outside of Halamshiral due to the machinations of Gaspard, they decide to join forces to find the
Dalish
and seek their aid in returning to Val Royeaux. On the way the party is savagely attacked by
sylvans
and Cheritenne as well as Celene's mount are slain, Cheritenne mercifully at Michel's hands. Clan Virnehn rescue them from the sylvans. When they reach the camp of Dalish clan Virnehn, they are treated with scorn and are told that the clan wants nothing to do with them. Michel is bound but later freed and lured by the
demon
Imshael
to the
elgar'arla
, the stone circle where
Keeper
Thelhen
keeps it imprisoned. Imshael reveals that it was summoned by the Keeper to help him activate the ancient
eluvians
. However, Imshael refused, as Thelhen only wants the eluvians awakened but nothing else; Imshael needed someone to make a choice. Imshael offers Michel a deal: it would
magically
grant Michel the valid identity of Ser Michel de Chevin, with no one ever finding out about him being elf-blooded. Imshael offers to magically alter other people's memories and forge documents to validate his fake heritage. All it wants in return is a choice, and a host, so that it could live outside
the Fade
.
Michel is soon found by Dalish warriors, who bring him back to the camp. When he reveals that it was Imshael who lured him away, Thelhen became alarmed and left to reinforce the binding circle. The Dalish warleader then accused Michel of endangering his clan. Michel silently indicated to Celene not to show weakness before the Dalish, so she requested that he allow the warleader a companion in the interest of a fair fight. Once the Dalish left them alone, Michel informed Celene of what he had learned from Imshael and they decided to take advantage of this information.
When Briala returned to the camp, they let her in on the secret. Though she believed they could use the information to gain favour with the Dalish, Celene convinced her that the Dalish are indifferent to the city elves and lied about their plans to kill her. Thus, Briala conceded to their plan to escape and left to convince Felassan to help them. Michel then kills several of the Dalish elves himself to free Celene. He spares the clan's First,
Mihris
, however, after she tells him he killed her love during the fight.
Returning to the binding circle, instead of accepting the terms of the offer, Michel tries to trick Imshael into giving him the keystone needed to activate the eluvians while not fulfilling his part of the bargain. When the demon puts down the keystone, Michel destroys its prison, believing that the demon would be forced to return to the Fade. However, by destroying the stone circle, he instead frees Imshael. Imshael goes on to massacre the rest of Clan Virnehn and, though Michel wants to turn back and stop Imshael, the group decide to leave the Dalish to their fate.
Using the keystone given to Celene by Imshael, Michel, Celene, Briala and Felassan enter into the
underground
chamber housing the nearest Eluvian, which Celene hopes to use to return to the capital ahead of Gaspard and end their conflict. The party eventually encounters Gaspard's entourage, however, which had been pursuing them with Mihris' help, and they agree to a temporary truce as they fight to survive in the distorted world and series of burial chambers to which the central chamber of the eluvians are connected. Though they are opposed, Michel prevents Celene from dishonorably murdering Gaspard during their journey.
After arriving at the central chamber, Ser Michel duels Gaspard to the death for the fate of Celene's kingdom. During the duel, Briala calls in her favor and asks Michel to yield to Gaspard instead of killing him. Michel is honor-bound to that promise and yields. This technically loses Celene's duel and, consequently, Michel's position as Celene's champion.
Briala, who now has control of the eluvians through the keystone, transports Michel and Gaspard outside of
Val Chevin
. The two men exchange words, Michel asking what would be his fate, knowing full well that the Academie would strip his name from the rolls and have him executed. However, Gaspard refuses to do so, stating that a strong character like Michel is an exemplar of what a chevalier should be, regardless of his blood line, comparing his example to that of
Ser Aveline
. He tells Michel to find his own path, as he would be executed if Celene lays eyes on him, and Gaspard refused to insult his honour by asking for his service. The two men then part ways. Michel, no longer Celene's champion, decides to dedicate the rest of his life to hunting and stopping Imshael to atone for releasing it.
Dragon Age: Inquisition
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Michel can be found just outside of
Sahrnia
, a town in
Emprise du Lion
. He tracked the demon
Imshael
to the nearby
Suledin Keep
, but with the town under threat from and the keep full of
Red templars
, he decided to stay there and protect the villagers instead of attacking the keep alone.
If
Vivienne
is in the active party she will remember who he is after he introduces himself, but explains that she didn't recognize him because he is dressed differently.
Cassandra Pentaghast
will ask further, after he introduces himself, if he is Ser Michel de Chevin, Empress Celene's champion, and Michel will reply, that he is no longer a champion and no longer "ser". If the Inquisitor asks further, he explains that he was champion, protector and perhaps once, even a friend, but now disgraced. The empress wants nothing to do with him and he cannot blame her. But despite all, he has a strong arm, a stout heart, and he still serves
Orlais
.
If Celene was killed during the quest
Wicked Eyes and Wicked Hearts
, the Inquisitor can tell him about her death. Michel will reply that the Game is merciless and that he wished he could have said goodbye. He even wonders, if he would have been able to protect her. Michel also states that
Gaspard de Chalons
will make a good emperor, in his own way.
Michel pledges himself to the
Inquisition
as an
agent
, if the
Inquisitor
kills the demon
Imshael
after talking to Michel outside Sahrnia. Michel will help fight a group of
Red Templars
in front of
Suledin Keep
, but will not follow the Inquisitor inside to fight Imshael, as he will need to return to Sahrnia to protect the people there who are being attacked by
Shades
unleashed by Imshael.
However, if the Inquisitor accepts a deal with Imshael, the demon will murder Michel.
If Imshael is slain prior to talking to Michel in Sahrnia, he can no longer be recruited for the Inquisition.
If Michel is recruited, the Inquisitor can later decide whether he will become a mentor to Inquisition soldiers, work with
Solas
on the
eluvians
or become a counselor for the nobility in
Lydes
. Michel will be seen walking
Skyhold
's courtyard.
If Gaspard becomes Emperor, either alone or ruling with Briala, he will offer Michel a full pardon for any prior incidents and a place in his honor guard. The Inquisitor may accept the offer or insist on keeping Michel.
Note:
Even if Michel returns to court under Emperor Gaspard, he will continue to provide his agent bonus at the
war table
.
Alternatively, if Celene is still Empress and Michel is an agent of the Inquisition, Celene will send Lady
Colombe
to try to negotiate a secret reconciliation between Celene and Michel. Celene cannot publicly forgive Michel due to her public reputation but she can still make use of him as a secret agent.
Leliana
suspects Celene's attempts at reconciliation is not truly out of magnanimity and she is merely using Michel as part of some scheme. The Inquisitor can undermine Celene's attempt to recruit Michel by stipulating Celene make the reconciliation public or allow Colombe to treat with Michel. If the latter is chosen—the reconciliation is successful, Lady Colombe acts as Michel and Celene's go-between, and Michel's mood is said to have improved.

Character
Minaeve

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Minaeve
is an elven mage scholar who serves as the head creature researcher for the reformed
Inquisition
in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Background
Minaeve was born into a
Dalish
clan. At the age of seven, she was cast out into the wilderness after displaying magical ability as her Dalish clan kept a limit on mages to avoid attracting too much attention. Shaken and malnourished, she eventually came upon a human village, but when the humans discovered her using magic to repel woodland predators, they attempted to kill her. The
templars
stepped in and she was taken to a mage
Circle
. Never particularly good at magic, Minaeve spent most of her time in the Circle studying as an apprentice. Minaeve speculates she was a year or so from undergoing her
Harrowing
. When her circle rebelled during the
Mage-Templar War
, Minaeve gathered a small group of
tranquil
and fled. Eventually, she and her wards found themselves under the protection of
Cassandra Pentaghast
, and when the Inquisition was reformed she signed on as head creature researcher.
Involvement
Minaeve can be found in
Haven
's chantry, in the same room as
Josephine
.
The Herald
can deliver enemy remains and place them on the table next to her for Minaeve to research.
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Minaeve dancing with
Seggrit
, celebrating the closing of
the Breach
During
Corypheus
's assault on Haven, Minaeve is pinned down alongside
Adan
next to a cart of combustible materials as a trail of fire approaches. If the Inquisitor fails to free her, she will be killed when the cart explodes. Whether or not she survives, when the Inquisition moves to
Skyhold
she is replaced by the tranquil mage
Helisma Derington
. If she survived, Minaeve can occasionally be found elsewhere in Skyhold; she mentions that she is focusing on her studies and directs the Inquisitor to Helisma.
Quests
Know Thy Enemy
In Your Heart Shall Burn
Quotes
Main article:
Minaeve/Dialogue
Codex entries
Black Wolf
Researcher
Trivia
A Dalish Inquisitor can tell Minaeve that
their clan
never abandoned children with magic, instead sending them to other clans,
a practice meant to ensure that no Dalish
Keeper
was without a successor and each clan had the guidance of one gifted with magic. This is the same reason why
Merrill
, originally born to the Alerion clan, was sent to the Sabrae clan.
Meanwhile,
Zathrian's clan
in
Dragon Age: Origins
had multiple mages present.

Mira
is an
Inquisition
guard stationed in
Skyhold
.
Background
Mira was a guard-captain for a noble named Lady Pendell. She joined the
Inquisition
after the incident at the
Divine Conclave
. Mira was present at
Haven
and saw
the Breach
. During the attack on
Haven
, she witnessed the Inquisitor fighting
Corypheus
and his
dragon
. Mira survived the fall of Haven and followed
the Inquisitor
to
Skyhold
.
Involvement
Mira can be encountered in Skyhold. If
Iron Bull
is recruited, he invites the Inquisitor to meet the regular soldiers fighting for the Inquisition, such as Mira and
Tanner
. The two guards are found in the Skyhold's courtyard, playing cards and drinking together. Iron Bull and the Inquisitor (disguised as
Grim
) approach them. After making the introduction, Iron Bull asks the guards about their perspective on the Inquisition. Mira tells them that she used to be a guard-captain for a noble lady. After what happened in Haven, she decided to help save the world. Mira also says that she doesn't sing the
Chant of Light
as much as she should, but the Inquisitor's brave stand against Corypheus gave her a reason to believe. After Iron Bull and the Inquisitor take their leave, Tanner and Mira continue the card game.

Background
When pressed by
the Inquisitor
for his qualifications for the crucial position of quartermaster, he lists noteworthy family connections all over
Thedas
, yet could name no qualifying trait for himself. He admits that even he questioned his own appointment to the position. His comments are carefully adjusted to avoid offense, such as noting that if the Inquisitor shares Threnn's views (on Teyrn Loghain) that they are "perfectly legitimate" views.
He states that his family has ties to several freehold militias, cousins "acting as officers" in Ferelden and Orlais, holds treaties with three new-money Tevinter houses (unspecified), and a rare Orzammar contract with a Paragon namesake (unspecified),
Involvement
Dragon Age: Inquisition
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
After
Corypheus
' assault on
Haven
, Morris will take over duties as quartermaster from
Threnn
. He can be found in a building marked "Quartermaster" on the map, located next to the armory. The building is not accessible until after the first time returning to Skyhold.
If Threnn survives the assault, Morris explains that the decision to replace her was made due to certain unpopular "views" she holds (likely referring to Threnn's favorable opinion of
Loghain Mac Tir
). Morris has an assistant, Ser Draman.
He will offer the
war table
operation
Negotiate a Deal for Weapon Plans
. He also participates in the operation
Outfitting the Crew
.

, meaning it may not follow some of the player's choices in the games.

Sutherland
recruited to investigate the silence of
Skyhold
's caretakers and its missing supply caravan. He participates in the fight against the Regret
demon
, formed out of
Solas
' murals, that successfully sends it back to
the Fade
.

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Movran the Under
is the chieftain of Edvarr Hold
, a tribe of
Avvar
people in the
Fallow Mire
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Movran's son, the
Hand of Korth
, was sent to kill
Tevinters
but decided that attacking the Herald of
Andraste
would bring more glory to his god. After his son's
death
, Movran answered, as is tradition in Avvar culture, by smacking the holdings of the offending party (in this case, the
Inquisitor
) with goat's blood. Movran freely admits, however, that he has no intention of actually pursuing any conflict with the
Inquisition
, and offers himself to the Inquisition for judgment. 
The Inquisitor may:
Banish Movran and his clan
Sentence Movran to be put in a gibbet (a hanging cage for public display)
Arm and exile Movran to the
Tevinter Imperium
Conscript Movran into the Inquisition, in which case he will serve alongside Lord
Esmeral Abernache
(only available if
Champions of the Just
was completed and Abernache survived)
If Movran is exiled to Tevinter, his clan will establish a settlement on an uninhabited region of the
Silent Plains
, off the
Imperial Highway
. The Inquisitor can either overtly support Movran's new settlement (incurring the Imperium's ire), covertly supply them (allowing the settlement to flourish and becoming a welcome stopping point along the road), or simply leave them to their own devices.
Alternatively, if partnered with Abernache and Josephine's suggestion is taken, Movran and Abernache develop something resembling a mutual grudging respect and become an effective ambassadorial team, with Josephine noting the value in the Inquisition's threat of "not recalling our ambassadors".

The Inquisitor may kill the Hand of Korth prior to the Inquisition's relocation to
Skyhold
. Even if this is the case, Movran will not retaliate for his son's death until after the Inquisition moves and the Herald of Andraste is proclaimed Inquisitor.

Character

Title

to Elindra

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Dragon Age: Inquisition multiplayer
Neria
is a player-controlled protagonist in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
's
multiplayer
.
Background
Neria was born into the
Ralaferin clan
, and was chosen as
Keeper
Elindra's apprentice. Trained from youth to defend and serve people, she takes great pride in her magic and her role as Elindra's
First
. Now within the
Inquisition
as a
Dalish
emissary, Neria does all she can to see that the interests of the Dalish are not forgotten amidst the chaos.
Chosen to be the Keeper's First at the age of nine, Neria takes her charge very seriously. She's viewed by others as thoughtful and focused.
Cillian
, her clanmate, once said of her, "Once she puts her mind to something, it must be done. It will be done."
Several years after she was made First, Neria attended the
Arlathvhen
with Elindra. Neria learned here that some of the other clans bore disrespect towards the Ralaferin clan. They believed that Elindra's predecessor,
Gisharel
, had harmed the Dalish when he shared Dalish lore and culture with human scholars. Neria argued in defense of her clan, but her conviction wavered. Upon returning from Arlathvhen, she had a long discussion with Elindra about Gisharel's actions. The conversation reinforced her loyalty and pride to her clan, believing that humans would only learn to respect the Dalish by seeing and understanding them. She now serves as not only an emissary of the Dalish within the Inquisition, but of the Ralaferin clan and their beliefs on foreign interaction.
Involvement
During the main game, Neria is involved in only one
war table
operation and can be seen often walking around Skyhold's
Garden
, though she cannot be spoken to.

Pala
is a player-controlled protagonist in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
's
multiplayer
.
Background
The
Silent Sisters
of
Orzammar
are an order of zealous female
dwarven
warriors who follow the example of
Paragon
Astyth
the Grey. Upon gaining membership into the order, each sister cuts out her own tongue to show her complete dedication to the art of war. When Pala learned of the
Inquisition
and its seemingly endless battle against
demons
, traitors, and monsters, the
dwarf
gladly accepted exile and the loss of her
caste
and become a
surfacer
.
Playstyle
Pala has a unique style that combines
warrior
and
rogue
abilities and traits, allowing her to rush into the front lines and strike multiple enemies at once. Like the
Katari
, Pala builds Guard on each hit, making her much more durable than other Damage specialists, particularly
Argent
and
Luka
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Pel Harmond
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Pel_Harmond
======================================================================

“We're the same,
you
and I. Well, that is overstating it. You are nothing like me.”
Character
Pel Harmond
Title
Lord
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Location
Verchiel
,
Orlais
Crestwood
,
Ferelden
Quests
A Battalion for Sera and Verchiel
The Verchiel March
Voice
Steven Kelly
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Lord
Pel Harmond
is a noble involved in a power struggle in the
Orlesian
city of Verchiel.
Background
According to the man himself, his family has ties to lower Ferelden militias across
Thedas
, which recently started to expand into Orlais. Whilst trying to "better his wealth and position", as he normally does, he came into a rivalry with Lady Chelle Morveau. Both were trying to take control of lands south of Verchiel, close to the
Dales
, and to have a chance at claim to the lands, both needed their own people to occupy the land. And so, Lord Harmond began forcing people to move out into the land, but then Lady Morveau would kick them out and move her own people in, and so forth.
Involvement
Sera
learns of the nobles' squabble over the land and how it affects the everyday people, and asked
the Inquisitor
for a small favour, involving the
Inquisition
soldiers marching through the town of Verchiel. If the Inquisitor agrees and allows their soldiers to march through the town, it puts Harmond's and Morveau's plans to waste as none can claim the land.
Upon hearing this news, some of the people affected ask Sera to meet them. However, it turns out to be a trap set up by Harmond, as he forced his servants under the threat of death to lure the infamous "
Red Jenny
" out in the open. He proceeds to kill Sera's informant, and then sics his mercenaries at Sera. Once his entourage is dead, Harmond realises that Sera came to the meeting with no other than the Inquisitor, and so he pleads to parley.
When talking to him, he will suggest an alliance between his family and Inquisition, much to the dislike of Sera. She warns the Inquisitor not to talk to Harmond. She can then be directed to kill him straight away, or Harmond can be either let go, or his lands can be acquired by the Inquisition via a Nobility Knowledge speech check. However, if the Inquisitor does speak to him, they can only ask him two out of four available questions before Sera loses her patience and beats Harmond to death.
Quests
A Battalion for Sera and Verchiel
(war table)
The Verchiel March
Trivia
The choice made regarding Harmond has no consequences. Neither acquiring his lands nor partnering up has any kind of effect, other than approval/disapproval from Sera.
Harmond is voiced by Steven Kelly, one of the winners of the
"Take Your Place in the Inquisition"
contest.
References

This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Philippe was assigned to protect the

Anton
and another guard about the Inquisitor, and is awaiting Grand Duke

in the

to hear a more detailed account of the Inquisition's fight against

and the
Archdemon
at
Haven
, which Philippe is very eager to hear, or, if the Inquisitor is
elven
, by convincing a few elven serving girls—which he'd mentioned finding very attractive—to distract Philippe and the other guard.

Celeste Thibault

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Lord
Pierren desRosier
is an
Orlesian
nobleman
.
Involvement
Pierren is a respected noble. Lady
Eustace Richelieu
, a matchmaker, wishes to arrange his marriage to
Celeste Thibault
, despite the considerable age difference and her wish to marry
Jecin Leandre
, believing it to be more profitable.
If the Inquisitor refuses to get involved:
Celeste Thibault and Jecin Leandre are killed when fighting breaks out between the desRosiers and Leandre families over the match. Lady Richelieu and Lord desRosiers can be found on the
Upper Level
of the
Summer Bazaar
in
Val Royeaux
, oblivious to Celeste's fate.
If the Inquisitor helps Celeste and Jecin elope:
Lady Richelieu and Lord desRosiers can be found on the
Upper Level
of the
Summer Bazaar
in
Val Royeaux
, oblivious about Celeste's fate.
If the Inquisitor helps Lady Richelieu arrange the marriage between Celeste and Lord desRosiers:
The Inquisitor can choose to attend the wedding ceremony, which is held on the
Upper Level
of the Summer Bazaar in Val Royeaux. Lady Richelieu will also be in attendance and she is surprised to find the Inquisitor attendance. Celeste questions whether they must do this; Lord Pierren tells her that it's for the families. When he sees that the Inquisitor is attending his wedding, Pierren says that he couldn't ask for more and welcomes them to speak at his wedding. Celeste tells Pierren to get it over with. The Inquisitor can bless the proceedings, either telling them to find purpose in duty or to marry for duty and love in secret. If the former, Lady Richelieu hints that she wishes to offer guidance, if not more, to Lady Celeste at court, but is told to shut up by the new bride. If the latter, Lady Celeste plans to reunite with Jecin as her lover, with the blessing of her new husband. Pierren says a standard arrangement and that he sees no reason to hold her youth hostage but he says that the idea was of Celeste. Lady Richelieu is not particularly pleased by this course of action. In either case, Lady Richelieu thanks the Inquisitor for coming to the wedding.

PAGE: Poulin

Character
Poulin
Title

Race

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Mistress
Poulin
is the leader of the town of
Sahrnia
in
Emprise du Lion
and owner of the nearby granite quarry.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
The mining trade which had long been a major source of income for Sahrnia collapsed due to the
War of the Lions
. To ease the economic strain, Mistress Poulin sold her family's quarry to the
Red Templars
, unaware that their true motives were to use the quarry to grow
red lyrium
. Eventually, the Red Templars demanded miners for the quarry. Knowing the Red Templars would likely kill her and take the villagers anyway if she refused, Poulin agreed and used the profits to sustain the citizens who remained.
She does not inform any authority about the situation in Sahrnia — including the
Inquisition
— when they arrive in the area to fight the templars.
Eventually, her treachery may be discovered by
the Inquisitor
when they assault the Red Templars at
Suledin Keep
as part of an offensive to secure
Emprise du Lion
. Poulin is imprisoned by the Inquisition and brought to
Skyhold
for
judgment
. The Inquisitor may:
Seize Poulin's financial assets for
House Trevelyan
(Human Inquisitor only)
Grant Poulin a pardon and release her
Sentence Poulin to hard labor
Execute Poulin
Have Poulin use her funds to rebuild Sahrnia (must have completed
Quarry Quandary
)
If Poulin is told to rebuild the town, she is grateful for the opportunity and later asks the Inquisition for aid in
moving
supplies to the town.
Quests
The Corruption of Sahrnia
Quarry Quandary
Sit in Judgment of Mistress Poulin
Judgment: Help the People of Sahrnia
(war table)
(conditional)
Note texts
Mistress Poulin's Records
Child's Diary
Notes
There is a reference to an "Alban Poulin" in the description of the
Sahrnia Quarry landmark
, but it's unclear whether this is a reference to Mistress Poulin or one of her relatives.

======================================================================
PAGE: Revered Mother (Inquisition)
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Revered_Mother_(Inquisition)
======================================================================

“They were her holiness's most trusted advisors. They represent her legacy, her hopes for peace in Thedas.”
Character
Revered Mother
Title
Revered Mother
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Affiliation
Orlesian Chantry
Location
Skyhold
Voice
Rachel Atkins
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
The
Revered Mother
is a member of the
Orlesian Chantry
. She can be found talking with
Josephine Montilyet
while in
Skyhold
.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
After
The Inquisitor
returns to Skyhold from the
Winter Palace
, the Revered Mother can be found in the courtyard with Josephine, insisting on having
Leliana
and
Cassandra
return to
Val Royeaux
as quickly as possible to attend ceremonies and ordinations. Josephine says that currently it's not possible for the other women to return, but she will attend to the matter as soon as possible. When she notices the Inquisitor, the Revered Mother asks to speak with them. She tells them that the end of the political turmoil has turned the Chantry to a single purpose: choosing the next
Divine
. She insists that it cannot be done without the Left and Right Hands of
Justinia V
. Josephine reiterates that Leliana and Cassandra cannot be spared from their duties, a statement that the Revered Mother meets with skepticism.
When the Inquisitor presses for more answers, they learn that Leliana and Cassandra stand as possible candidates to be the next Divine. The Revered Mother goes on to explain that while they aren't candidates
yet
, the Chantry needs them to be as they may be able to rally the clerics and gain a consensus of votes. She also explains there is precedent for those outside the clergy being chosen as Divine to break a deadlock.
Whatever the Inquisitor replies with, the Revered Mother will push for Leliana and Cassandra to be sent to Val Royeaux. Josephine then interjects, excusing herself and the Inquisitor from the conversation. The Revered Mother bows and leaves, presumably returning to Val Royeaux.

Haven
to await the
Divine
Conclave's outcome; when the
temple
was destroyed, his hope for resolution was lost. Rion signed up with the
Inquisition
; seeing it as the mages' last chance for peace.

that was tampering in
blood magic
. The Herald can either promote her from scout to covert agent, whereby Ritts' talents would be put to better use or inform the worried scout that she is safe and optionally tell him of her actions while she was on duty.
Note:
If the confrontation with the attackers goes on for too long, Ritts will eventually get killed. If the path up the hill is taken rather than the nearby tower, ambushing the attackers will allow for Ritts to potentially stay alive for the duration of the confrontation. If the quest is completed prior to recruiting Ritts, the option to recruit her as an agent will no longer be available.

======================================================================
PAGE: Roderick Asignon
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Roderick_Asignon
======================================================================

For the character from
Dragon Age II
, see
Roderick
.
“Mock if you will. I'm certain the Maker is less amused.”
Character
Roderick Asignon
Title
Grand Chancellor of the
Chantry
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Affiliation
Orlesian Chantry
Location
Haven
Quests
The Wrath of Heaven
The Threat Remains
In Your Heart Shall Burn
Voice
Christopher Godwin
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Roderick Asignon
is the Grand Chancellor of the
Chantry
in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Roderick is a bureaucrat responsible for communicating the
Divine
's will to the rest of the Chantry. He also handles correspondence for the Divine, spreads her word to Thedas and is her advisor on mundane matters.
As such, despite his relatively low position in the Chantry hierarchy compared to the clergy, he enjoys a considerable amount of influence. Following the eruption of the
Breach
and the destruction of the conclave between the
mages
and
templars
, every Chantry official who outranked Roderick was killed, leaving him the de facto head of the organization while the surviving
grand clerics
convene the Grand Consensus to elect a new Divine.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Roderick is first encountered just after the Breach erupts in
Haven
. He is stationed at the forward camp and immediately distrusts the
Inquisitor
, as well as
Cassandra Pentaghast
and
Leliana
for supporting them. He demands that the Inquisitor to be sent to
Val Royeaux
to be tried and executed, believing them responsible for the Breach and the loss of life ensued. With the chain of command in chaos, Roderick attempted to assert his authority to force a retreat, but Cassandra chose to defer to the Inquisitor and the party pressed towards the Temple of Sacred Ashes.
While the Inquisitor is unconscious after stabilizing the Breach, Roderick starts arguing with Cassandra in
Haven
's Chantry. The Chancellor, still convinced of the Inquisitor's guilt despite their efforts, insists that they be sent to Val Royeaux to be tried. However, Cassandra believes that the Inquisitor and the mark on their hand were the key to resolving the crisis and invokes a writ by the late
Divine Justinia V
, declaring the reformation of the
Inquisition
, and declaring that they will find the perpetrators behind the Breach and restore order, with or without Chantry approval. Subsequently, Roderick uses his influence to have many of the surviving clerics brand the fledgling Inquisition a heretical movement for harbouring the Inquisitor, who had been labeled the Herald of
Andraste
.
Shortly after the Inquisition gains the power to address the clerics in Val Royeaux, Roderick returns to Haven in the middle of a dispute between the Inquisition's mages and templars, which
Cullen
has to diffuse. The chancellor offers nothing but pessimism to the Inquisition's efforts.
When Haven is attacked by
Corypheus
, Roderick is mortally wounded in the attack, having attempted to fight off a Venatori or Red Templar in order to save a villager. With what little strength he had left, Roderick reveals the existence of a secret pathway for the Inquisition to escape. Before parting ways with the Inquisitor, he expresses his change in opinion of them. When the Inquisition makes it to safety, Roderick quietly succumbs to wounds in the makeshift camp.
When conversed with, Cole tells the Inquisitor that Roderick had deeply regretted his transgressions against them and came to admire them in his final moments.
Quests
The Wrath of Heaven
The Threat Remains
In Your Heart Shall Burn
Quotes
(Believing the Inquisitor is responsible)
"As grandmaster of the Chantry, I hereby order you to take this criminal to Val Royeaux to face execution."
(After sealing the Rift at the Temple)
"Have you gone completely mad? The prisoner failed, Seeker. The Breach is still in the sky. For all you know, he/she intended it this way.)
(Before the Inquisitor travels to Val Royeaux)
"Better ready yourself for the blame you will be rightly assigned."
Codex entries
High Chancellor Roderick

Runa Lyrsdotten
is an
Avvar
from
Stone-Bear Hold
in the
Frostback Basin
.
Background
Runa is an avid mountain-climber; her climbing sites can be seen all across the Frostback Basin.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
The Inquisitor
is asked to go looking for Runa by her cousin
Linna
, who says that she can most likely be found climbing in the hills. The Inquisitor can find signs of Runa's passage all over the Frostback Basin. They find her on top of the hill, being attacked by a
gurgut
. Once she's safe, Runa will explain that she got carried away, feeling as if a spirit was helping her along.
Runa will proceed to give thanks to the spirit at a nearby shrine, and propose to include the Inquisitor's name in her prayer in thanks for their help. The Inquisitor can accept or decline.

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Knight-Captain
Rylen
is an
Inquisition
commander stationed at
Griffon Wing Keep
and
Cullen
's second-in-command.
Background
Rylen is the youngest of five children of a
Starkhaven
stonemason. He joined the
Templar Order
at fifteen because he wanted to do something useful with his life. He quickly gained a reputation as a problem solver among Starkhaven's Templars, and eventually became Knight-Captain.
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age II
.
Following the destruction of the
Kirkwall
chantry in 9:37
Dragon
, Rylen was dispatched to lead an aid mission and coordinate rescue efforts. While in Kirkwall, he met Cullen leading the remnants of Kirkwall's Templars.
When the
Mage-Templar War
broke out,
Knight-Commander Carsten
elected to follow
the Lord Seeker
's edict, and joined the revolt against the
Chantry
. Rylen and many of the other senior Templar officers dissented and refused to follow. When Cullen offered them a position within the Inquisition, Rylen and many of his loyalists chose to join.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Knight-Captain Rylen is first mentioned during the Herald of Andraste's first private conversation with Cullen. As they talk, an Inquisition soldier runs up to Cullen and informs him of Ser Rylen's report regarding supplies. Rylen may also be involved in
Truth or Dare: The Imperial Court
war table
operation, where he escorts nobles to the remains of the
Temple of Sacred Ashes
. Later on, he can be found in person on the upper-most level of Griffon Wing Keep after
the Inquisitor
captures the Griffon Wing Keep
.
When the Inquisitor takes Griffon Wing Keep from the hands of the
Venatori
, Rylen takes over as commander of the fort, coordinating reports from the Inquisition's agents in the area. The Inquisitor can consult Knight-Captain Rylen on the status of Keep.

saarebas

Ben-Hassrath

Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Trespasser
.
Saarath once was an ashkaari (i.e., a scholar, or scientist), spending his days examining the philosophy of the
Qun
and instructing others in it. When his
magic
manifested, he became a saarebas under the command of
Viddasala
. He was involved in the study of the
Veil
on her orders, a part of the Qunari plan called "Dragon's Breath".

This section contains spoilers for:
Trespasser
.
The Inquisitor catches a glimpse of Saarath and Viddasala entering an
eluvian
in the Gully within
Elven Ruins
. If
Cole
is present, he explains that Saarath can't be far from her lest he feels pain.
In the Shrine to the Dread Wolf,
Viddasala
orders Saarath to attack
the Inquisitor
; but he manages to break free of his leash in the course of the fight and flees.
Saarath later confronts the Inquisitor in a secluded area within the Shrine where he guards a single
eluvian
. His mask is now half-broken, magic crackles around him and he summons
demons
to aid him in battle. The Inquisitor weakens Saarath and then
uses the Anchor
to kill him.

Background
Seanna is the daughter of Master Dennet,

This section contains spoilers for:

.
The Herald
goes looking for Master Dennet in the hopes of securing his horses for the
Inquisition
. However, he will not send them to the Inquisition until his lands are safe and he's confident that his animals will be well-cared for. He gifts The Herald a horse from his stables and directs them to see his daughter Seanna, who has prepped the horse for them. She offers to set up three courses around the farm allowing for the Herald to get acclimated with riding a stead. If the Herald completes them within the allotted time, she rewards them with some coin that she was saving for herself.

Character
Seryl
Title

Here Lies the Abyss

Dragon Age: The Masked Empire

Dragon Age: Inquisition
(mentioned)
Lady Seryl of Jader
is an Orlesian noblewoman and the ruler of Jader, a strategic port city on the coast of the
Waking Sea
. She is a steadfast loyalist to
Empress Celene Valmont I
.
Background
As the governing lady of Jader, Seryl manages the primary gateway between
Orlais
and
Ferelden
. Her city is culturally significant as one of the sites claiming to be the birthplace of the prophet
Andraste
.
During her tenure, she established a close working relationship with Mother
Giselle
, who served as the Revered Mother of Jader's Chantry. Together, they addressed the humanitarian crises—including famine and disease—caused by the influx of Fereldan refugees following the
Fifth Blight
. Lady Seryl worked closely with Mother Giselle, then the Revered Mother of Jader’s Chantry.
During the aftermath of the Fifth Blight,
Jader
was overwhelmed by Fereldan refugees, leading to famine and disease. While the Chantry in
Val Royeaux
demanded food be distributed based on social hierarchy, Mother Giselle refused and, with Seryl’s backing, provided relief to all in need regardless of race or status.
Involvement
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: The Masked Empire
.
Seryl ordered the destruction of villages surrounding Jader. This tactic was designed to deny Gaspard's troops shelter (billeting) and intimidate local peasants into withholding support from the rebels.
She utilized "scorched earth" tactics to protect Empress
Celene
's interests, ordering the destruction of villages where Grand Duke
Gaspard
's troops might seek shelter to deter local peasants from aiding the rebellion.
After being ambushed at
Halamshiral
, Celene and Ser
Michel de Chevin
initially attempted to flee to
Jader
, trusting Seryl to provide a secure base to rally their forces. However, Gaspard's scouts blocked the western highway, forcing the Empress to divert to
Val Royeaux
.
Dragon Age: Inquisition
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Lady Seryl acts as a bridge for the Inquisition’s influence in the Orlesian port city of Jader. Shortly after the Inquisition establishes itself at
Skyhold
, Chantry loyalists in Jader begin spreading rumors that the Inquisitor was responsible for the death of Divine
Justinia V
.
While the operation focuses on silencing these rumors through the Inquisitor's advisors, it occurs within Seryl's jurisdiction, maintaining
Jader
as a stable loyalist stronghold for the Inquisition's cause.
Seryl's supply of trebuchets and heavy machinery allows the
Inquisition
to breach the gates and occupy the Wardens, providing the Inquisitor with a clear path to confront Warden-Commander
Clarel de Chanson
and the magister
Livius Erimond
. As the Inquisition prepares to assault the ancient Grey Warden fortress of Adamant in the
Western Approach
, Lady Seryl provides the necessary modern siege equipment.
Quests
Here Lies the Abyss

This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Tevinter Nights
.
The plot follows BioWare's own canon
, meaning it may not follow some of the player's choices in the games.
Callback
Shayd, now known as Ser Shayd, Lady of Evesol, accompanies
Sutherland
to
Skyhold
to investigate the loss of contact with its caretakers and a missing supply caravan. Inside the rotunda, they are confronted by a Regret
demon
that took shape from the plaster of
Solas
' murals to the
Inquisitor
. When the demon uses regret to briefly neutralize her, Shayd thinks back to when she was fourteen, running through an alley in Dales End. She thinks back to the cruel words she spoke, though doesn't reveal what those were.
Shayd is freed from the demon's influence when
Dagna
throws a
jar of bees
at it. She later participates in the fight that successfully sends the demon back to the
Fade
.

“Plan or no plan, if you die, I get your corpse”
Character
Sidony
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Class
Mage
Specialization

Affiliation
Mortalitasi
Inquisition

Zoe Telford
Appearances
Heroes of Dragon Age
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Dragon Age: Inquisition multiplayer
Dragon Age: Tevinter Nights
Sidony
is a player-controlled protagonist in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
's
multiplayer
.
Background
Sidony was born in
Nevarra
. When her magic manifested, she was cast away by her mother. Sidony doesn't remember how old she was at the time, nor how long she wandered the streets of Nevarra City until she was found by a
Mortalitasi
mage
, Lord Henrik, who began training her in secret.
Sidony was brought up to revel in her magical abilities. She feels no kinship with mages who do not share her pride, and she has little but disdain for most other people. Sidony's only goal is to uncover her true potential as a mage, so she hungers for magical knowledge. When news of
The Breach
reached her, she headed directly to see it for herself, hoping that whatever secrets it held would be the key to her advancement.
Involvement
Sidony is involved in various
war table
operations. Though she can sometimes be seen on the battlements with two other agents, near where
Cullen
is stationed, she can't be spoken to.
Dragon Age: Tevinter Nights
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: Tevinter Nights
.
The plot follows BioWare's own canon
, meaning it may not follow some of the player's choices in the games.
Murder by Death Mages
Cassandra Pentaghast
orders Sidony to return to
Nevarra City
to investigate rumors of a Mortalitasi plot to assassinate a member of
Nevarra
's unstable line of succession. Upon her return, Sidony finds out that her former mentor, Lord Henrik, the man who tipped the Inquisition of the plot, has been murdered. Eventually, Sidony discovers that Nicolas Reinhardt attempted to frame her for the murders of several nobles to cause backlash against the Mortalitasi, while the Mortalitasi mage Antonia killed Henrik and used her to uncover Reinhardt's plot to strengthen the Mortalitasi. Sidony kills Reinhardt and Antonia in retaliation.

“Titles outside the royal family are not recognized at court, but they remain part of ancient estates.”
Character
Solange Montbelliard
Title
Comtesse
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Affiliation
Council of Heralds
Location
Winter Palace
Quests
Wicked Eyes and Wicked Hearts
Dance with the Dowager: The Courante
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Comtesse
Solange Montbelliard,
also known as
the Silver Lady of Churneau
, is an
Orlesian
noblewoman
and a member of the
Council of Heralds
.
Background
Vivienne
once helped Comtesse Solange when she attracted unwanted attention from a
Nevarran
ambassador, writing on behalf of the Comtesse that she "only likes men with self-respect."
Leliana
calls her "the Silver Lady of Churneau" and suggests she could be a worthy ally.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
As a member of the
Council of Heralds
, Comtesse Solange is attending the peace talks between
Celene Valmont I
,
Briala
and
Gaspard de Chalons
to end the
War of the Lions
. She can be found in the
Lower Garden
, which can be accessed by using three
halla statues
, with her fellow council members,
Lothaire Doucy
and
Cyril de Montfort
. If
Varric Tethras
is brought along to the
Winter Palace
, Solange and Lothaire will comment on his writing.
At the entrance of the Winter Palace, the Inquisitor can encounter a noblewoman distraught over the loss of her ring, which she says was a gift from Comtesse Montbelliard. They can choose to return the ring to her or keep it for themselves.
The Inquisitor
can discuss the purpose of the Council of Heralds with Solange. She explains that noble titles are not officially recognized by the court —aside from those used by the royal family. However, the historical titles are still significant in Orlesian society, serving as a reminder of the ancient lineages. Solange says that if there is no clear inheritor to an estate, then it's the Council's duty to decide who should receive it. This conversation unlocks the codex
Codex entry: Council of Heralds
. The Inquisitor can ask Solange if she has noticed anything strange; she will mention that the royal wing of the palace is sealed and nobody knows why.
After the peace talks, Solange can use her position on the Council to
help
the
Inquisition
claim the disputed region of the Ylenn Basin, including all its revenues and oaths, over Comte Poisson.
Quests
Wicked Eyes and Wicked Hearts
Dance with the Dowager: The Courante
(war table)
Note texts
A Letter to an Ambassador
Notes
Dance with the Dowager: The Courante
misspells her surname as
Montebelliard
.
References

PAGE: Storyteller

URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Storyteller
======================================================================

“These statues come from ancient dreams of blood and bones, lost to the memory of man. Be wary of them.”
Character
Storyteller
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Location
Redcliffe Village
,
Hinterlands
Quests
A Spirit in the Lake
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
The
Storyteller
can be found in the
Hinterlands
, standing near a large statue located in
Redcliffe Village
.
Involvement
The Storyteller can be heard saying that no man needs statues so great as those whose remnants lie toppled in the hills and that the statues come from ancient dreams of blood and bones lost to the memory of man. She says to be wary of them.
The Inquisitor
can ask her about the people of Redcliffe and its history. She tells the Inquisitor that a spirit dwells in a small lake south of the highway. She also says that the girls of the village bring daisies to it, asking for love, but that the spirit rarely answers because it is a spirit of valor that favors
blood lotus
flowers and not a spirit of love.

A Spirit in the Lake

======================================================================
PAGE: Surgeon
CATEGORIES: Characters, Dragon Age: Inquisition characters
URL: https://dragonage.fandom.com/wiki/Surgeon
======================================================================

Character
Surgeon
Title
Surgeon
Race
Human
Gender
Female
Location
Skyhold
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
The
Surgeon
was one of the refugees in the camps near
Skyhold
until
Cullen Rutherford
brought her to the
Inquisition
to help the sick and injured.
Involvement
The Surgeon can initially be found in
Skyhold
's courtyard, helping injured soldiers and civilians. She's very busy and states that she should focus on the wounded, but takes some time to tell
the Inquisitor
how she's been helping the pilgrims in simple ways, setting broken bones and performing simple amputations. When the Inquisitor further asks about the injured, she replies that there's fewer by the day, as some heal while others pass away. She tries to make their passing painless. However, the most grievously wounded never made it to Skyhold in the first place.
The Inquisitor can also ask her whether healing shouldn't be left up to
mages
, but she retorts that good health isn't magic, but science, and depends on diet, exercise and a balance of the humors.
If the Inquisitor chooses to build the
Infirmary Courtyard
Upgrade in Skyhold, the Surgeon will move to the newly built infirmary.
Trivia
The Surgeon believes in
Humorism
. Essentially, this theory holds that the mortal body is filled with four basic substances, called humors, which are in balance when a person is healthy. All diseases and disabilities supposedly result from an excess or deficit of one of these four humors. These deficits were thought to be caused by vapors inhaled or absorbed by the body. The four humors are black bile, yellow bile, phlegm, and blood. Treatments from this school of thought are bloodletting and the application of leeches.

Dragon Age: Inquisition
-
Jaws of Hakkon
Svarah "Sun-Hair" Janesdotten
is the Thane of the
Avvar
of
Stone-Bear Hold
, located in the
Frostback Basin
.
Background
Svarah won her
legend-mark
'Sun-Hair' for a battle in which her hair was set aflame by an enemy archer. Cornered by other opponents, she had no time to put out the flame, earning her the epithet which she wears to this day. Since then she has ruled Stone-Bear Hold with temperance and wisdom. Svarah has little love for the
Jaws of Hakkon
, feeling their pronounced warlike nature can only end in disaster but maintains a diplomatic if cold relationship with
Gurd Harofsen
and their neighbouring Avvar.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Svarah first encounters
the Inquisitor
when they come seeking permission to visit the island on the nearby lake, which is held sacred by the Avvar of Stone-Bear Hold. Svarah grants them permission to go, but refuses to join the
Inquisition
in combat against the Hakkonites due to an existing treaty between the two holds, as well as the threat of other Avvar holds the Hakkonites have allied with retaliating. Svarah also requests that the Inquisitor aid them in their search for
Storvacker
, their sacred Hold-Beast who has recently vanished.
Upon discovering that the Hakkonites were responsible for Storvacker's abduction and that they planned to sacrifice her for a ritual, Svarah becomes enraged at their betrayal and readily pledges to aid the Inquisition in their battle with the Jaws of Hakkon. Svarah rallies Stone-Bear Hold to assist in assaulting the
Old Temple
where the Hakkonites are based. Their combined forces are enough to put an end to them. Afterwards, if the Inquisitor has completed
Guests of the Hold
, Svarah bestows them with a
legend-mark
(a ritual epithet among the Avvar), naming them Inquisitor First-Thaw.

======================================================================

Character
Tanner
Title
Guard
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Affiliation
Inquisition
Location
Skyhold
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Tanner
is an
Inquisition
guard stationed in
Skyhold
.
Background
Before joining the Inquisition, Tanner was a farmer who lived in the countryside near
Jader
. After the explosion at the
Divine Conclave
, he was inspired to join the
Inquisition
and signed up as a guard. There, he met and befriended
Mira
, a fellow guard.
Involvement
Tanner can be encountered in
Skyhold
when
Iron Bull
invites
the Inquisitor
to meet some of the regular soldiers fighting for the Inquisition, such as Tanner and Mira. Iron Bull and the Inquisitor (disguised as
Grim
) join the two guards as they play cards and drink in Skyhold's courtyard. Bull asks them their perspective on the Inquisition. Tanner says that he didn't want to spend his whole life as a farmer and that he "needed to live a little". After Iron Bull and the Inquisitor take their leave, Tanner and Mira resume their card game.

Notes
Although Taven's name is spelled "Taven" when he introduces himself and when he is referred to in dialogue by other characters, his in-game model's name is spelled and reads "Tavin".

of

Character
Telana
Race
Elf

(

)

Dalish

Dragon Age: Inquisition
-
Jaws of Hakkon
(mentioned)
Telana
is an
elven
dreamer
mage
who had the love and affection of
Inquisitor
Ameridan
.
Background
A few pages barely legible from an old torn book describe Ameridan and Telana's final moments together:
As
Haron
and
Orinna
drew the
Avvar
that were guarding
the fortress
away, Telana and Ameridan painstakingly managed to destroy the
Tevinter
frost-ward that sealed its entrance—as the Avvar's mastery of
ice
allowed them to slip through the ward without melting it.
The plan entailed luring
the dragon
into a trap once inside. However, the Avvars managed to fend them off and put up a brutal fight as the dragon's power was like none either of the two had ever seen. Possessed by the Avvar
god-spirit
—which rivaled that of the legendary
Archdemon
Dumat
—the beast managed to severely injure Telana in the ensuing confrontation.
Telana claimed that she could continue on fighting, but despite their use of healing magic, her limp spoke louder than words. Ameridan thought it best to send Telana back outside, as his final act would be to unleash a powerful
spell
to seal the dragon within the fortress forever. Knowing just how small her chance for escape would be in her current state, he waited as long as he could, praying that she escaped the ruins in time to warn Orinna and Haron—then bound himself to Hakkon for all eternity.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
The Inquisitor
discovers that Telana escaped from the fortress and ended up on a nearby
island
. She went to sleep in an attempt to see Ameridan once more through her
dreams
. However, she couldn't find him and then perished of her injuries. In death, she attracted the attention of numerous
spirits
, some of which identified with her so strongly that they preserved not just her belongings but some of her memories as well.
When the Inquisitor meets Ameridan, they can either tell him Telana's true fate or lie to him and say that she escaped and went on to live well.

Trivia
Telana is also the name of a character in the earlier BioWare game,
Baldur's Gate II
.

The Augur
is an
Avvar
from
Stone-Bear Hold
in the
Frostback Basin
.
Background
His title of Augur indicates that he is Stone-Bear Hold's resident
mage
leader, responsible for interpreting the will of the Gods and handling all matters of the arcane. On their first meeting, he introduces
the Inquisitor
to a host of
spirits
with which he is seen conversing.
Involvement
The Inquisitor can ask the Augur about the
strange artifacts
from the swamp produced by the
Jaws of Hakkon
. Before he explains their purpose, the Augur first asks that the Inquisitor familiarize themselves with Avvar magic and beliefs by reading nearby
Veilfire
runes (which took him months to carve). He then explains that the
Jaws of Hakkon
are using the magic of bones to hide themselves from the other gods, which they have all spurned in favor of
Hakkon Wintersbreath
.
The Augur also helps in
investigating
his apprentice;
Sigrid Gulsdotten
. He explains that he did not exile her, but that she exiled herself when she couldn't release her spirit teacher. Eventually, the Inquisitor can choose to convince Sigrid to go to the Augur for guidance, or recruit her for the
Inquisition
.

Character
Thornton
Race
Human
Gender
Male

Rogue

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Dragon Age: Inquisition multiplayer
Thornton
is a player-controlled protagonist in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
's
multiplayer
.
Background
A veteran ranger from
Ansburg
in the
Free Marches
, Thornton first served as a soldier in the Margrave of Ansburg's army, quickly finding a knack for stealth and reconnaissance. He became a valued scout, whose information resulted in the success of several key campaigns and quick thinking ensured his survival behind enemy lines. According to him, he eluded capture through various means, concealing himself in trees, pretending to be rock formations, hiding in burning buildings, running through fields of venomous snakes, and in his favorite tale, disguising himself as a general's wife so perfectly as to fool the general.
Thornton eventually moved to
Orlais
and obtained a position in the Orlesian army. When the
Orlesian Civil War
erupted, he fought on the side of Empress
Celene
until he was sent to the
Temple of Sacred Ashes
in the
Frostback Mountains
as support for the
Divine Conclave
.
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
In the wake of the Conclave's destruction and the reestablishment of the
Inquisition
, Thornton joined the Inquisition to lend his expertise in the hope of restoring order to
Thedas
.
Involvement
Thornton is involved in a
war table
operation. Though he can sometimes be seen on the battlements at
Skyhold
with two other agents, near where
Cullen
is stationed, he can't be spoken to.

Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Threnn
is the
Inquisition
's quartermaster at
Haven
in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Background
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Origins
.
Before joining the Inquisition, Threnn served with
Loghain Mac Tir
's forces at
Ostagar
during the
Fifth Blight
. She has expressed a view of Loghain's innocence, and believes that King
Cailan
over-extended his forces and the signal fire was lit too late by
the Warden
and
Alistair
. Threnn escaped with the rest of Loghain's forces.
If
Anora
remains queen of Ferelden and is ruling alone or alongside Alistair, Threnn will state that Anora took pity on her because of Threnn's loyalty to Loghain, Anora's father, and so sent her to either help or hinder the Inquisition, depending on the World State.
If Alistair was made king of Ferelden and rules alone or alongside the Warden, Threnn will state that he sent her to the Inquisition to simply get rid of her.
Involvement
Threnn serves as the quartermaster for the Inquisition and is in charge of the requisitions.
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
During the
assault
of Haven, Threnn is seen fighting either
Red Templar
or
Venatori
forces. If the Herald fails to help her, she will fall. If she survives, she joins the rest of the Inquisition in
Skyhold
, though she no longer serves as the quartermaster. She can be found walking around in various locations.
Eustace Morris
takes on the quartermaster role, and says it was thought best Threnn be replaced with someone more politically palatable, now that they are in Orlais.
If Loghain was made a
Grey Warden
she will comment on going to give him her respects when he comes to
Skyhold
, and the fact that he even remembered her name. She reiterates that he was "the best commanding officer this world has ever seen."

“You have done much, but have you the stomach for... the Quizquisition?”
Character
Trifles Minutiae
Title
Lord
Race
Human
Gender
Male
Affiliation
Inquisition
Location
Skyhold
Voice
David Schofield
Appearances
Dragon Age: Inquisition
Lord
Trifles Minutiae
is a confusing nobleman who ostensibly resides at
Skyhold
and periodically appears in various places to interrogate
the Inquisitor
regarding historical trivia. He claims this is part of the 'Quizquisition'. Answering three of these questions correctly awards
the Boon of the Spoon
.
Quizquisition
Questions are randomly selected from the following:
Name the
Archdemon
of the
First Blight
.
Dumat
Name the Archdemon of the
Fifth Blight
.
Urthemiel
Loghain Mac Tir
was teyrn of which Fereldan settlement?
Gwaren
Chantry
belief centers on the enigmatic
Maker
and
His Bride
. Name her... traitorous husband.
Maferath
The extermination of
nugs
in
Kirkwall
is known as...?
Battle of Squealing Plains
Thedas
's largest city?
Minrathous
The
Qunari
are guided by a very particular philosophy. Name its author.
Koslun
Possible locations
Lord Trifles Minutiae can randomly be found at various places throughout Skyhold:
In the basement vault (near the kitchen) - Requires the
Elite Clientele
perk
.
On the upper floor of
Herald's Rest
, near the exit across from
Cole
.
Near the stables.
In the closet of the Inquisitor's chambers.
At the top of the mage/Templar tower.
In the first cell of the dungeons. (Bugged, see below)
Near the front gate, on the ledge to the right.
On the rooftop near the ramp leading to the kitchen. Accessed by climbing the broken East Wall section behind the stables, then jumping down; or leave Leliana's tower by the door to the outside, follow the wall to the end, and jump down onto the kitchen roof top.
In the last of three rooms that are accessed from Vivienne's "room" - Requires completing a main story quest for the scaffolding blocking the way to be removed.
Notes
Lord Trifles seems to appear most frequently in the basement vault location.
If the Inquisitor takes too long to answer, he interrupts, stating that the time has run out.
Trivia
Trifles and Minutiae are semantically related when it comes to topics pertaining to trivia.
Bugs
It is possible to save after correctly answering Lord Trifles Minutiae's first question, then load that save in order to answer a second and third question at the same location. Saving after correctly answering the third question, then loading that save to answer the third question again can result in receiving another spoon (can be done a maximum of five times).
As of
Patch 5
, it is nearly impossible to interact with Trifles at his location in the dungeons on console. It might be possible to interact with him by walking through the door of the cell and jumping multiple times.
Before you unlock the
Elite Clientele
perk
, he can be stuck in the unopened vault. You can see his outline through the painting on the wall, or the icon to talk to him through the stones below the stairs up to the main hall.

Character

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Troilus Hertubise
was an amateur researcher who came to the
Emerald Graves
to investigate
the Breach
.
Background
Troilus came from the town of
Lydes
. When The Breach opened up in the sky, he found the rifts it opened so interesting that he decided to study them. In his diary, he refered to the rifts as "the Menace", and called investigating them his "Great Mission". He took interest in the
Rifts at the Pavilion
. When he approached one of them, it was inactive. He assumed his studies of the rifts would allow him to close it. However, he failed and ultimately died at his camp near the rift.
Involvement
The Inquisitor
can find Troilus'
diaries
, as well as his corpse.

Dragon Age: Inquisition
Valorin
is a
Dalish
elf from
Keeper
Hawen
's clan.
Background
Valorin was a young
mage
studying under Keeper Hawen's tutelage, whose teachings he found frustratingly slow. Shortly before his seventeenth birthday, Valorin was passed over for the position of Keeper's First in favor of
Taven
. He ran away from the camp shortly after, eager to prove his worth.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for
:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
When
The Inquisitor
reaches the
Dalish Encampment
on the
Exalted Plains
, they can meet
Emalien
, Valorin's older sister. She is concerned about her brother, whose current whereabouts are unknown, and fears the worst. She asks the Inquisitor to look for Valorin.
The Inquisitor can find Valorin's burnt corpse near a ruined house. The remains of his journal tell the truth of what happened: Valorin decided to retrieve
Lindiranae
's talisman from the
Shrine to Sylaise
to prove that he deserved to be First. However, as the talisman was sealed behind magical wards that he couldn't break on his own, Valorin ventured into the nearby
war zone
, where
the Veil
was thin, and attempted to summon
demons
through a
blood magic
ritual. The ritual went wrong and Valorin was killed.
When the Inquisitor returns to the Dalish Encampment, they can either tell Emalien that her brother was brave, that he was stupid, or that he used blood magic. They can also choose to complete Valorin's mission by retrieving the talisman themselves. Giving the talisman to Emalien earns them even more
favor
from the Dalish clan.
Quests
Someone to Lose
Something to Prove
Note texts
Valorin's Journal
Trivia
Valorin received his
vallaslin
before the age of seventeen; the design he chose is unknown.

Character

Title

Lady
Velise Thibault
is an
Orlesian
noblewoman
and the matriarch of House Thibault in
Dragon Age: Inquisition
. As a prominent "new money" figure in Val Royeaux, where she navigates the cutthroat political landscape of the Orlesian Imperial Court.
Background
Velise Thibault is a pragmatic matriarch focused on elevating her family's status in the cutthroat environment of the Imperial Court. The Thibaults are considered "upstarts" by established noble houses, having built their fortune through trade and mercantile success rather than ancient lineage. Velise is the mother of
Celeste Thibault
, whom she views as the family's most valuable asset for securing a permanent place among the Orlesian elite.
Velise is dedicated to securing her family's long-term standing, primarily through the strategic marriage of her daughter, Celeste Thibault.
Involvement
Dragon Age: Inquisition
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
Velise enters the Inquisition's orbit when House Thibault becomes embroiled in a political rivalry with House desRosier. The conflict, known as the "Alliances" chain, requires the
Inquisitor
to choose a side, with Velise representing the more progressive, trade-oriented faction.
She requests The Inquisitor to intervene in the rivalry between the Thibaults and the desRosiers but a major turning point occurs when
Jecin Leandre
, who is in love with Celeste, protests her arranged marriage to the much older Lord
Pierren desRosier
.
She sends her letters to the Inquisitor, Velise remains pragmatic, stating her daughter will comply with the family's needs but urging that the resulting power benefit the Thibaults rather than external matchmakers like Lady
Richelieu
.

rare oil and ambers merchant.
Background
Vicinius was born in the settlement of Tallo, though he claims to be from Vyrantium. By 9:41
Dragon
, he has become a wealthy merchant.
Involvement
This section contains spoilers for:
Dragon Age: Inquisition
.
If the
Templars
were recruited:
The Inquisition
is attacked by the

, led by

In
his notebook
, he states that he called a meeting with Calpernia right before the meeting with the Inquisition, to demand a compensation for branding his men. However, Calpernia had different plans. She ordered the Venatori to kill him for mistreating slaves.
